<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"> </h2><a id="user-content--1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  " href="#-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">
<code>$PATH</code> contains incompatible directory paths</h3><a id="user-content-path-contains-incompatible-directory-paths" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: $PATH contains incompatible directory paths" href="#path-contains-incompatible-directory-paths"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>By default, Termux exports only termux bin path(s) <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin</code> in the <code>$PATH</code> variable for Android <code>&gt;= 7</code> and <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin:/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/applets</code> for Android <code>&lt; 7</code>, but not the <code>/system/bin</code> path for Android system bin path, since normally, users should only use termux provided binaries.</p>
<p>If system provided binaries need to be executed, then <code>/system/bin</code> can be either be set or appended at end of <code>$PATH</code>, like <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin:/system/bin</code>.</p>
<p>However, if Termux app is using <strong><a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element#target" rel="nofollow"><code>targetSdkVersion</code></a> <code>&gt;= 29</code> with the <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-exec/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/technical/index.md#app-data-file-execute-restrictions"><code>termux-exec</code> <code>system_linker_exec</code></a> workaround</strong> and a system command under <code>/system/bin</code> is executed and <strong><code>$PATH</code> is set to or contains <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin</code> before <code>/system/bin</code></strong>, then commands may fail. Termux provides wrappers under <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin</code> for some system commands, like for <code>/system/bin/cmd</code>. (<a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-tools/blob/v1.40.1/scripts/Makefile.am#L47-L59">1</a>, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-tools/blob/v1.40.1/scripts/Makefile.am#L83-L93">2</a>) If the utilities like <code>/system/bin/am</code>, <code>/system/bin/pm</code> and <code>/system/bin/settings</code> that run <code>cmd</code> command themselves are executed <strong>without <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> being set</strong>, then <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin/cmd</code> wrapper will attempted to be executed instead of the real <code>/system/bin/cmd</code>, which will fail with the <code>Permission denied</code> error and a <a href="https://source.android.com/docs/security/features/selinux/validate" rel="nofollow">SeLinux <code>avc</code> denied</a> message will be logged in <a href="https://developer.android.com/tools/logcat" rel="nofollow"><code>logcat</code></a>, like <code>avc:  denied  { execute_no_trans } for  path="/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/cmd" dev="dm-55" ino=46573 scontext=u:r:untrusted_app:s0:c29,c257,c512,c768 tcontext=u:object_r:app_data_file:s0:c29,c257,c512,c768 tclass=file permissive=0 app=com.termux</code> due to <a href="https://github.com/agnostic-apollo/Android-Docs/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/apps/processes/app-data-file-execute-restrictions.md"><code>App Data File Execute Restrictions</code></a> for <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin/cmd</code> being engaged. For example, if <code>out="$(LD_PRELOAD= /system/bin/pm path com.termux 2&gt;&amp;1 &lt;/dev/null)"; echo "$out"</code> is executed. However, if <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> was set to <code>termux-exec</code>, then it would hook the <code>exec()</code> call to bypass the restriction, but that's generally not advisable to be set when running system commands. See also <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-tools/commit/be50057f"><code>termux/termux-tools@be50057f</code></a>.</p>
<p><strong>To prevent such issues</strong>, make sure termux bin paths do not exist in <code>$PATH</code> when running system binaries, like by:</p>
<ul>
<li>Setting it manually in current process environment before running the command with <code>PATH=/system/bin</code>.</li>
<li>Setting it temporarily for a single command with <code>LD_LIBRARY_PATH= LD_PRELOAD= PATH=/system/bin command [args...]</code>.</li>
<li>Use <a href="https://github.com/agnostic-apollo/tudo/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/usage/index.md#path-and-ld_library_path-priorities"><code>tudo</code></a> and <a href="https://github.com/agnostic-apollo/sudo/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/usage/index.md#path-and-ld_library_path-priorities"><code>sudo</code></a> commands with the <code>-A</code> or <code>-AA</code> flags.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"> </h2><a id="user-content--2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  " href="#-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">App Data File Execute Restrictions</h3><a id="user-content-app-data-file-execute-restrictions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: App Data File Execute Restrictions" href="#app-data-file-execute-restrictions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>If Termux app is running on Android <code>&gt;= 10</code> and <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/v0.118.0/gradle.properties#L19">uses</a> <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element#target" rel="nofollow"><code>targetSdkVersion</code></a> <code>&gt;= 29</code>, then as part of Android <code>W^X</code> restrictions with the <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/_/android/platform/system/sepolicy/+/0dd738d810532eb41ad8d90520156212ce756648" rel="nofollow"><code>0dd738d8</code></a> commit via <a href="https://source.android.com/docs/security/features/selinux" rel="nofollow">SeLinux</a> policies, it will not be able to <code>exec()</code> its app data files, like under the <code>/data/data/&lt;package_name&gt;</code> (for user <code>0</code>) directory.</p>
<p>Check <a href="https://github.com/agnostic-apollo/Android-Docs/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/apps/processes/app-data-file-execute-restrictions.md"><code>App Data File Execute Restrictions</code> android docs</a> for more information on the <code>W^X</code> restrictions, including that apply to other app domains.</p>
<p>Check <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-exec/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/technical/index.md#app-data-file-execute-restrictions"><code>termux-exec</code> <code>App Data File Execute Restrictions</code></a> docs for more info on a working workaround using <code>system_linker_exec</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"> </h2><a id="user-content--3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  " href="#-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Linux vs Termux <code>bin</code> paths</h3><a id="user-content-linux-vs-termux-bin-paths" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Linux vs Termux bin paths" href="#linux-vs-termux-bin-paths"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>If binaries under <code>/bin</code> or <code>/usr/bin</code> directories or scripts with <code>/bin/*</code> or <code>/usr/bin/*</code> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shebang_(Unix)" rel="nofollow">shebang</a> interpreter paths are executed without <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-exec"><code>termux-exec</code></a> being set in <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code>, they will either fail to execute with <code>No such file or directory</code> errors or will execute the android system binaries under <code>/system/bin/*</code> (as <code>/bin</code> is a symlink to <code>/system/bin</code>) if the same filename exists, instead of executing binaries under the Termux <code>bin</code> path <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin</code>. Check <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-exec/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/technical/index.md#linux-vs-termux-bin-paths"><code>termux-exec</code> <code>Linux vs Termux </code>bin<code> paths</code></a> and <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-tasker#termux-environment"><code>termux-tasker</code> <code>Termux Environment</code></a> docs for more info.</p>
<hr>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element">Dynamic Library Linking</h2><a id="user-content-dynamic-library-linking" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dynamic Library Linking" href="#dynamic-library-linking"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>The <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dynamic_linker" rel="nofollow">dynamic linker</a> is the part of the operating system that loads and links the shared libraries needed by an executable when it is executed. The kernel is normally responsible for loading both the executable and the dynamic linker. When a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Exec_(system_call)" rel="nofollow"><code>execve()</code> system call</a> is made for an <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Executable_and_Linkable_Format#Program_header" rel="nofollow"><code>ELF</code></a> executable, the kernel loads the executable file, then reads the path to the dynamic linker from the <code>PT_INTERP</code> entry in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Executable_and_Linkable_Format#Program_header" rel="nofollow"><code>ELF</code> program header table</a> and then attempts to load and execute this other executable binary for the dynamic linker, which then loads the initial executable image and all the dynamically-linked libraries on which it depends and starts the executable. For binaries built for Android, <code>PT_INTERP</code> specifies the path to <code>/system/bin/linker64</code> for 64-bit binaries and <code>/system/bin/linker</code> for 32-bit binaries. The <code>ELF</code> file headers can be checked with the <a href="https://www.man7.org/linux/man-pages/man1/readelf.1.html" rel="nofollow"><code>readelf</code></a> command, like <code>readelf --program-headers --dynamic /path/to/executable</code>.</p>
<p>For Android, libraries are opened and loaded by the system linker (<code>/system/bin/linker[64]</code>) as per the following order. Check <a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages/ld.so.8.en.html" rel="nofollow"><code>ld.so</code></a> and <a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages-dev/dlopen.3.en.html" rel="nofollow"><code>dlopen</code></a> man page and Android system linker source (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=2209" rel="nofollow">1</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=1837" rel="nofollow">2</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=1610" rel="nofollow">3</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=1477" rel="nofollow">4</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=1351-1362" rel="nofollow">5</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=1039" rel="nofollow">6</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=1160" rel="nofollow">7</a>) for more info.</p>
<ul>
<li>If library name contains a path separator <code>/</code> like for a relative or absolute path, then it is attempted to be directly opened.</li>
<li>Else if library name does not contain a path separator <code>/</code>, then following directory paths are searched in-order non-recursively for file with the same <a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages-dev/basename.3.en.html" rel="nofollow"><code>basename</code></a> as the library name:
<ul>
<li>The directory paths in the <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> environment variable.</li>
<li>The directory paths in the <code>DT_RUNPATH</code> dynamic section attribute of the binary, if present, but only for library dependency is listed as <code>DT_NEEDED</code>.</li>
<li>The <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=102-125" rel="nofollow">default system library paths</a> like <code>/system/lib64</code>, <code>/system/lib</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Note that for android, if full library path contains <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker_utils.cpp;l=138" rel="nofollow"><code>!/</code></a>, then system linker assumes that the library file may exist inside a <code>zip</code>/<code>apk</code> file and will attempt to open the library inside the <code>zip</code> file before opening full library path itself. (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=999-1001" rel="nofollow">1</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=914" rel="nofollow">2</a>). For example <code>/path/to/foo.apk!/lib/arm64/bar.so</code> would open the <code>lib/arm64/bar.so</code> library inside the <code>/path/to/foo.apk</code> <code>apk</code> file.</p>
<p>The <code>DT_RPATH</code> dynamic section attribute of the binary and the <code>ld</code> cache file (<code>/etc/ld.so.cache</code>) like other systems is not used.</p>
<p>For info on dynamic linking errors, check <a href="#dynamic-library-linking-errors">Dynamic Library Linking Errors</a> section below.</p>
<p>For info on <code>$PATH</code>, <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code>, <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> environment variables exported by Android and Termux for execution and dynamic linking, check <a href="#path-environment-variables">Path Environment Variables</a>, <a href="#path-environment-variables-exported-by-android">Path Environment Variables Exported By Android</a>, <a href="#path-environment-variables-exported-by-termux">Path Environment Variables Exported By Termux</a>.</p>
<hr>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element">Dynamic Library Linking Errors</h2><a id="user-content-dynamic-library-linking-errors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dynamic Library Linking Errors" href="#dynamic-library-linking-errors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>If opening, loading and linking the library fails, then the system linker will generate error the <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker_main.cpp;l=257" rel="nofollow"><code>CANNOT LINK EXECUTABLE</code></a> error, with sub errors like <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=1351-1362" rel="nofollow"><code>library &lt;library&gt; not found</code></a> and <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker_relocate.cpp;l=121" rel="nofollow"><code>cannot locate symbol &lt;symbol&gt; referenced by &lt;executable/dependency_library&gt;</code></a>, etc. Following are the possible reasons in Termux for linker errors.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#package-dependencies-are-outdated">Package dependencies are outdated</a></li>
<li><a href="#ld_library_path-contains-incompatible-directory-paths"><code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> contains incompatible directory paths</a></li>
<li><a href="#system-libraries-are-missing">System Libraries are missing</a></li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Package dependencies are outdated</h3><a id="user-content-package-dependencies-are-outdated" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Package dependencies are outdated" href="#package-dependencies-are-outdated"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>Termux packages use a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rolling_release" rel="nofollow">rolling release</a> update model. All packages must be upgraded together and partial upgrades are not supported in Termux, which are supported on some other Linux distributions.</p>
<p>If a package is upgraded and its dependency packages are not, then linker errors may trigger. This is because the updated package may be requiring different libraries or different symbols in libraries than the one provided by the old dependency library currently installed. So all executables and their dependency libraries may require being upto date to be compatible.</p>
<p><strong>To prevent or fix such issues, upgrade all packages.</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pkg upgrade"><pre>pkg upgrade</pre></div>
<p>The <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-tools/blob/90ff1a7a/scripts/pkg.in#L341"><code>pkg</code> command is a wrapper script</a> in Termux around the <a href="https://wiki.debian.org/Apt" rel="nofollow"><code>apt</code></a> or <a href="https://wiki.archlinux.org/title/pacman" rel="nofollow"><code>pacman</code></a> package managers, depending on the package manager being used by the user in the Termux rootfs.</p>
<p>The <code>pkg</code> command depends on <code>curl</code>, so if <code>curl</code> gets broken, then instead run <code>apt update &amp;&amp; apt full-upgrade</code> if using <code>apt</code> and <code>pacman -Syu</code> if using <code>pacman</code>.</p>
<p>If <code>apt</code> or <code>pacman</code> itself gets broken, then their package and dependency <code>deb</code>/<code>tar</code> files will have to be manually downloaded from the <a href="https://packages.termux.dev/apt/termux-main/pool/main" rel="nofollow">termux <code>main</code> packages repository</a> and then installed. Otherwise, <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX</code> can be deleted or the Termux app reinstalled, but that will result in all Termux package data being lost and will require reinstalling packages again, though <code>$HOME</code> can be preserved if just deleting <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"> </h2><a id="user-content--4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  " href="#-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">
<code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> contains incompatible directory paths</h3><a id="user-content-ld_library_path-contains-incompatible-directory-paths" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: $LD_LIBRARY_PATH contains incompatible directory paths" href="#ld_library_path-contains-incompatible-directory-paths"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>As detailed in above sections:</p>
<ul>
<li>Android <code>&gt;= 7</code>, the <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> variable must not contain <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib</code> or <code>/system/lib[64]</code> paths.</li>
<li>Android <code>&lt; 7</code>, the <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> variable must only contain <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib</code> when executing a termux executable under <code>$TERMUX__ROOTFS</code>, and must not contain <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib</code> or <code>/system/lib[64]</code> paths when executing an android provided executable, like under <code>/system</code> partition.</li>
</ul>
<p>This is because if <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> is set, then the wrong library may be selected by the linker when searching instead of as per <code>DT_RUNPATH</code> or default system libraries. <strong>To fix this</strong>:</p>
<ul>
<li>Do not set <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> in the environment, like with shell rc files (<code>~/.bashrc</code>, <code>~/.profile</code>, etc).</li>
<li>Unset it in the current process environment before running the command with <code>unset LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code>.</li>
<li>Just unset it temporarily for a single command with <code>LD_LIBRARY_PATH= command [args...]</code>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Unsetting both <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> and <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> is especially necessary for android system commands under <code>/system/bin</code></strong>, like with <code>LD_LIBRARY_PATH= LD_PRELOAD= command [args...]</code>, the termux provided wrappers under <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin</code> for some system commands already do this. (<a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-tools/blob/v1.40.1/scripts/Makefile.am#L47-L59">1</a>, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-tools/blob/v1.40.1/scripts/Makefile.am#L83-L93">2</a>) The <a href="https://github.com/agnostic-apollo/tudo/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/usage/index.md#path-and-ld_library_path-priorities"><code>tudo</code></a> and <a href="https://github.com/agnostic-apollo/sudo/blob/master/site/pages/en/projects/docs/usage/index.md#path-and-ld_library_path-priorities"><code>sudo</code></a> commands can also be used with the <code>-A</code> or <code>-AA</code> flags.</p>
<p>The <code>ffmpeg</code> executable is one example for this. Check <a href="#listing-and-searching-libraries-and-symbols">Listing and Searching Libraries and Symbols</a> docs for info on the helper functions used below.</p>
<p>The termux <code>ffmpeg</code> depends on system provided <code>libgui.so</code>, which recursively depends on system provided <code>libEGL.so</code> itself. If <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> contains <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib</code>, then the wrong termux provided <code>libEGL.so</code> library from the <code>libglvnd</code> package at <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libEGL.so</code> would get selected instead of the system provided one at <code>/system/lib64/libgui.so</code>, which will not contain the required <code>eglDestroySyncKHR</code> symbol, causing a linker error.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ LD_LIBRARY_PATH=&quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib&quot; ffmpeg
CANNOT LINK EXECUTABLE &quot;ffmpeg&quot;: cannot locate symbol &quot;eglDestroySyncKHR&quot; referenced by &quot;/system/lib64/libgui.so&quot;...
$ LD_LIBRARY_PATH=&quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib:/system/lib64:/system/lib&quot; ffmpeg
CANNOT LINK EXECUTABLE &quot;ffmpeg&quot;: cannot locate symbol &quot;eglDestroySyncKHR&quot; referenced by &quot;/system/lib64/libgui.so&quot;...

$ search_dynamic_symbol &quot; eglDestroySyncKHR&quot; 3
/system/lib64/libEGL.so
000000000001b5cc T eglDestroySyncKHR
--
/system/lib/libEGL.so
000130e8 T eglDestroySyncKHR

$ list_library_dependencies &quot;/system/lib64/libgui.so&quot; 1 | grep libEGL
        libEGL.so =&gt; /system/lib64/libEGL.so

$ dpkg -S &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libEGL.so&quot;
libglvnd: /data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libEGL.so

$ list_dynamic_symbols &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libEGL.so&quot; | grep &quot; eglDestroySyncKHR&quot;"><pre>$ LD_LIBRARY_PATH=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$TERMUX__PREFIX</span>/lib<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ffmpeg
CANNOT LINK EXECUTABLE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ffmpeg<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: cannot locate symbol <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>eglDestroySyncKHR<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> referenced by <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib64/libgui.so<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>...
$ LD_LIBRARY_PATH=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$TERMUX__PREFIX</span>/lib:/system/lib64:/system/lib<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ffmpeg
CANNOT LINK EXECUTABLE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ffmpeg<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: cannot locate symbol <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>eglDestroySyncKHR<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> referenced by <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib64/libgui.so<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>...

$ search_dynamic_symbol <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> eglDestroySyncKHR<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 3
/system/lib64/libEGL.so
000000000001b5cc T eglDestroySyncKHR
--
/system/lib/libEGL.so
000130e8 T eglDestroySyncKHR

$ list_library_dependencies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib64/libgui.so<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep libEGL
        libEGL.so =<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> /system/lib64/libEGL.so

$ dpkg -S <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$TERMUX__PREFIX</span>/lib/libEGL.so<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
libglvnd: /data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libEGL.so

$ list_dynamic_symbols <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$TERMUX__PREFIX</span>/lib/libEGL.so<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> eglDestroySyncKHR<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<p>The termux <code>ffmpeg</code> depends on termux provided <code>libavformat.so</code> from the <code>ffmpeg</code> package, which recursively depends on termux provided <code>libssh.so</code> itself from the <code>libssh</code> package. If <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> contains <code>/system/lib64:/system/lib</code>, then the wrong system provided <code>libssh.so</code> library at <code>/system/lib64/libssh.so</code> would get selected instead of the termux provided one at <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libssh.so</code>, which will not contain the required <code>sftp_read</code> symbol, causing a linker error.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$ LD_LIBRARY_PATH=&quot;/system/lib64:/system/lib&quot; ffmpeg
CANNOT LINK EXECUTABLE &quot;ffmpeg&quot;: cannot locate symbol &quot;sftp_read&quot; referenced by &quot;/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libavformat.so.60.3.100&quot;...

$ search_dynamic_symbol &quot;sftp_read@&quot; 3
/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libssh.so
000000000005b81c T sftp_read@@LIBSSH_4_5_0

$ list_library_dependencies &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libavformat.so&quot; 1 | grep libssh
        libssh.so =&gt; /data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libssh.so

$ dpkg -S &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libavformat.so&quot;
ffmpeg: /data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libavformat.so

$ dpkg -S &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libssh.so&quot;
libssh: /data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libssh.so

$ search_dynamic_library libssh.so 3
/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libssh.so
/system/lib64/libssh.so"><pre>$ LD_LIBRARY_PATH=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib64:/system/lib<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ffmpeg
CANNOT LINK EXECUTABLE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>ffmpeg<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>: cannot locate symbol <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>sftp_read<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> referenced by <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libavformat.so.60.3.100<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>...

        libssh.so =<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> /data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libssh.so

<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"> </h2><a id="user-content--5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  " href="#-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">System Libraries are missing</h3><a id="user-content-system-libraries-are-missing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: System Libraries are missing" href="#system-libraries-are-missing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>Termux packages may depend on android system libraries that are considered stable APIs by <code>NDK</code>. These vary depending on Android version, and can be checked by reading <code>/system/etc/public.libraries.txt</code> on a specific device. Check <code>NDK</code> (<a href="https://developer.android.com/ndk/guides/stable_apis" rel="nofollow">Stable APIs docs</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/_/android/toolchain/prebuilts/ndk/r26/+/6dae871c87da3f0f798c1d848ad6b7ba83343d43:meta/system_libs.json" rel="nofollow"><code>meta/system_libs.json</code></a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/_/android/toolchain/prebuilts/ndk/r26/+/6dae871c87da3f0f798c1d848ad6b7ba83343d43:build/core/system_libs.mk" rel="nofollow"><code>build/core/system_libs.mk</code></a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/_/android/toolchain/prebuilts/ndk/r26/+/6dae871c87da3f0f798c1d848ad6b7ba83343d43:build/cmake/system_libs.cmake" rel="nofollow"><code>build/cmake/system_libs.cmake</code></a>), system core (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:system/core/rootdir/etc/public.libraries.android.txt" rel="nofollow"><code>/etc/public.libraries.android.txt</code></a>), system linker (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:frameworks/libs/native_bridge_support/linker/linker_translate_path.cpp;l=57-129" rel="nofollow"><code>linker_translate_path.cpp</code></a>), and <code>ART</code> (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:art/tools/buildbot-build.sh;l=357-399" rel="nofollow"><code>buildbot-build.sh</code></a>) for more info.</p>
<p>The libraries are assumed to exist on all Android devices depending on Android version, but may not exist on emulated Termux environments, like <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-docker"><code>termux-docker</code></a>. This causes linker errors for certain packages if a required library is not available.</p>
<p>For example, <code>ffmpeg</code> executable depends on <code>libandroid.so</code>, which isn't available in <code>termux-docker</code> and requires installing the <code>libandroid-stub</code> package to be able to execute the <code>ffmpeg</code> command. The <code>libandroid-stub</code> package installs a stub version of the library at <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libandroid.so</code>, which also does not depend on any other system libraries. Check <code>libandroid-stub</code> package <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/blob/master/packages/libandroid-stub/build.sh"><code>build.sh</code></a>, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/commit/f3043a2e"><code>f3043a2e</code></a>, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/commit/807c36d1"><code>807c36d1</code></a>, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/pull/16680"><code>termux/termux-packages#16680</code></a> and <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/pull/16902"><code>termux/termux-packages#16902</code></a> for more info.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# /etc/public.libraries.android.txt
# See https://android.googlesource.com/platform/ndk/+/master/docs/PlatformApis.md

<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element">Listing and Searching Libraries and Symbols</h2><a id="user-content-listing-and-searching-libraries-and-symbols" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Listing and Searching Libraries and Symbols" href="#listing-and-searching-libraries-and-symbols"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>The following methods can be used after exporting them in a <code>bash</code> shell to list and search libraries or their symbols. Copy and paste them in the terminal or <a href="https://www.gnu.org/software/bash/manual/html_node/Bash-Builtins.html#index-source" rel="nofollow"><code>source</code></a> them, like by adding them to <code>~/.bashrc</code> and starting a new interactive <code>bash</code> shell.</p>
<p>For the <code>search_*</code> methods, the <code>mode</code> parameter should be between <code>1-3</code> inclusive.</p>
<ul>
<li>If <code>1</code> is passed, only <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX</code> paths are searched.</li>
<li>If <code>2</code> is passed, only <code>/system/lib[64]</code> paths are searched.</li>
<li>If <code>3</code> is passed, both <code>$TERMUX__PREFIX</code> and <code>/system/lib[64]</code> paths are searched.</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# search_dynamic_library library_name_regex mode [additional_grep_options]
search_dynamic_library() {
local library=&quot;$1&quot;; local mode=&quot;$2&quot;; shift 2;
[ -z &quot;$library&quot; ] &amp;&amp; { echo &quot;library not passed.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1; };
case &quot;$mode&quot; in ''|*[!1-3]*) echo &quot;mode '$mode' passed is invalid. It must be between 1-3.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1;;esac
local -a paths=();
{ [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;1&quot; ] || [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;3&quot; ]; } &amp;&amp; paths+=(&quot;${TERMUX__PREFIX:-$PREFIX}&quot;);
{ [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;2&quot; ] || [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;3&quot; ]; } &amp;&amp; { [ -d &quot;/system/lib64&quot;  ] &amp;&amp; paths+=(&quot;/system/lib64&quot;); paths+=(&quot;/system/lib&quot;); };
find &quot;${paths[@]}&quot; -name &quot;*.so&quot; -print 2&gt;/dev/null | grep -E &quot;$@&quot; -- &quot;$library&quot;
}

# search_static_library library_name_regex mode [additional_grep_options]
search_static_library() {
local library=&quot;$1&quot;; local mode=&quot;$2&quot;; shift 2;
[ -z &quot;$library&quot; ] &amp;&amp; { echo &quot;library not passed.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1; };
case &quot;$mode&quot; in ''|*[!1-3]*) echo &quot;mode '$mode' passed is invalid. It must be between 1-3.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1;;esac
local -a paths=();
{ [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;1&quot; ] || [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;3&quot; ]; } &amp;&amp; paths+=(&quot;${TERMUX__PREFIX:-$PREFIX}&quot;);
{ [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;2&quot; ] || [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;3&quot; ]; } &amp;&amp; { [ -d &quot;/system/lib64&quot;  ] &amp;&amp; paths+=(&quot;/system/lib64&quot;); paths+=(&quot;/system/lib&quot;); };
find &quot;${paths[@]}&quot; -name &quot;*.a&quot; -print 2&gt;/dev/null | grep -E &quot;$@&quot; -- &quot;$library&quot;
}


# search_dynamic_symbol symbol_name_regex mode [additional_nm_options]
search_dynamic_symbol() {
local symbol=&quot;$1&quot;; local mode=&quot;$2&quot;; shift 2;
[ -z &quot;$symbol&quot; ] &amp;&amp; { echo &quot;symbol not passed.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1; };
case &quot;$mode&quot; in ''|*[!1-3]*) echo &quot;mode '$mode' passed is invalid. It must be between 1-3.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1;;esac
local -a paths=();
{ [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;1&quot; ] || [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;3&quot; ]; } &amp;&amp; paths+=(&quot;${TERMUX__PREFIX:-$PREFIX}&quot;);
{ [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;2&quot; ] || [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;3&quot; ]; } &amp;&amp; { [ -d &quot;/system/lib64&quot;  ] &amp;&amp; paths+=(&quot;/system/lib64&quot;); paths+=(&quot;/system/lib&quot;); };
{ while IFS= read -r -d '' lib; do echo &quot;$lib&quot;; nm --dynamic --extern-only --defined-only --demangle &quot;$@&quot; -- &quot;$lib&quot; 2&gt;/dev/null | grep -E -- &quot;$symbol&quot; | grep -v &quot; U &quot;; done &lt; &lt;(find &quot;${paths[@]}&quot; -name &quot;*.so&quot; -print0 2&gt;/dev/null); } | grep -E -B 1 -- &quot;$symbol&quot;
}

# search_static_symbol symbol_name_regex mode [additional_nm_options]
search_static_symbol() {
local symbol=&quot;$1&quot;; local mode=&quot;$2&quot;; shift 2;
[ -z &quot;$symbol&quot; ] &amp;&amp; { echo &quot;symbol not passed.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1; };
case &quot;$mode&quot; in ''|*[!1-3]*) echo &quot;mode '$mode' passed is invalid. It must be between 1-3.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1;;esac
local -a paths=();
{ [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;1&quot; ] || [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;3&quot; ]; } &amp;&amp; paths+=(&quot;${TERMUX__PREFIX:-$PREFIX}&quot;);
{ [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;2&quot; ] || [ &quot;$mode&quot; = &quot;3&quot; ]; } &amp;&amp; { [ -d &quot;/system/lib64&quot;  ] &amp;&amp; paths+=(&quot;/system/lib64&quot;); paths+=(&quot;/system/lib&quot;); };
{ while IFS= read -r -d '' lib; do echo &quot;$lib&quot;; nm --demangle --defined-only &quot;$@&quot; -- &quot;$lib&quot; 2&gt;/dev/null | grep -E -- &quot;$symbol&quot; | grep -v &quot; U &quot;; done &lt; &lt;(find &quot;${paths[@]}&quot; -name &quot;*.a&quot; -print0 2&gt;/dev/null); } | grep -E -B 1 -- &quot;$symbol&quot;
}


# list_dynamic_symbols library_path [additional_nm_options]
list_dynamic_symbols() {
local library=&quot;$1&quot;; shift 1;
[ -z &quot;$library&quot; ] &amp;&amp; { echo &quot;library not passed.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1; };
nm --dynamic --extern-only --defined-only --demangle &quot;$@&quot; -- &quot;$library&quot;
}

# list_static_symbols library_path [additional_nm_options]
list_static_symbols() {
local library=&quot;$1&quot;; shift 1;
[ -z &quot;$library&quot; ] &amp;&amp; { echo &quot;library not passed.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1; };
nm --demangle --defined-only &quot;$@&quot; -- &quot;$library&quot;
}


# list_library_dependencies library_path recursive
list_library_dependencies() {
local library=&quot;$1&quot;; local recursive=&quot;$2&quot;; shift 2;
[ -z &quot;$library&quot; ] &amp;&amp; { echo &quot;library not passed.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1; };
case &quot;$recursive&quot; in ''|*[!0-1]*) echo &quot;recursive '$recursive' passed is invalid. It must be 0 or 1.&quot; 1&gt;&amp;2; return 1;;esac
if [ &quot;$recursive&quot; = &quot;0&quot; ]; then readelf --dynamic -- &quot;$library&quot; | grep -F &quot;(NEEDED)&quot;  | sed -E 's/^.*Shared library: \[(.*)\]$/\1/'; else ldd -- &quot;$library&quot;; fi
}"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> search_dynamic_library library_name_regex mode [additional_grep_options]</span>
<span class="pl-en">search_dynamic_library</span>() {
<span class="pl-k">local</span> library=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">local</span> mode=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$2</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">shift</span> 2<span class="pl-k">;</span>

}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> search_static_library library_name_regex mode [additional_grep_options]</span>
<span class="pl-en">search_static_library</span>() {
<span class="pl-k">local</span> library=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">local</span> mode=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$2</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">shift</span> 2<span class="pl-k">;</span>
