}


<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> search_dynamic_symbol symbol_name_regex mode [additional_nm_options]</span>
<span class="pl-en">search_dynamic_symbol</span>() {
<span class="pl-k">local</span> symbol=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">local</span> mode=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$2</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">shift</span> 2<span class="pl-k">;</span>
[ <span class="pl-k">-z</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$symbol</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> { <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>symbol not passed.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1<span class="pl-k">;</span> }<span class="pl-k">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>|<span class="pl-k">*</span>[!1-3]<span class="pl-k">*</span>) <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>mode '<span class="pl-smi">$mode</span>' passed is invalid. It must be between 1-3.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1;;<span class="pl-k">esac</span>
<span class="pl-k">local</span> -a paths=()<span class="pl-k">;</span>
{ [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]<span class="pl-k">;</span> } <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> paths+=(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${TERMUX__PREFIX<span class="pl-k">:-</span><span class="pl-smi">$PREFIX</span>}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)<span class="pl-k">;</span>
{ [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]<span class="pl-k">;</span> } <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> { [ <span class="pl-k">-d</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib64<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>  ] <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> paths+=(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib64<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)<span class="pl-k">;</span> paths+=(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)<span class="pl-k">;</span> }<span class="pl-k">;</span>
{ <span class="pl-k">while</span> IFS= <span class="pl-c1">read</span> -r -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> lib<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$lib</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> nm --dynamic --extern-only --defined-only --demangle <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$@</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$lib</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span>/dev/null <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -E -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$symbol</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -v <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> U <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;(</span>find <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${paths[@]}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -name <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>*.so<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -print0 <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span>/dev/null<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> } <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -E -B 1 -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$symbol</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> search_static_symbol symbol_name_regex mode [additional_nm_options]</span>
<span class="pl-en">search_static_symbol</span>() {
<span class="pl-k">local</span> symbol=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">local</span> mode=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$2</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">shift</span> 2<span class="pl-k">;</span>
[ <span class="pl-k">-z</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$symbol</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> { <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>symbol not passed.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1<span class="pl-k">;</span> }<span class="pl-k">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>|<span class="pl-k">*</span>[!1-3]<span class="pl-k">*</span>) <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>mode '<span class="pl-smi">$mode</span>' passed is invalid. It must be between 1-3.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1;;<span class="pl-k">esac</span>
<span class="pl-k">local</span> -a paths=()<span class="pl-k">;</span>
{ [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]<span class="pl-k">;</span> } <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> paths+=(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${TERMUX__PREFIX<span class="pl-k">:-</span><span class="pl-smi">$PREFIX</span>}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)<span class="pl-k">;</span>
{ [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$mode</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>3<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]<span class="pl-k">;</span> } <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> { [ <span class="pl-k">-d</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib64<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>  ] <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> paths+=(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib64<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)<span class="pl-k">;</span> paths+=(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/system/lib<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)<span class="pl-k">;</span> }<span class="pl-k">;</span>
{ <span class="pl-k">while</span> IFS= <span class="pl-c1">read</span> -r -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> lib<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$lib</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> nm --demangle --defined-only <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$@</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$lib</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span>/dev/null <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -E -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$symbol</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -v <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> U <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;(</span>find <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${paths[@]}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -name <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>*.a<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -print0 <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span>/dev/null<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> } <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -E -B 1 -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$symbol</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}


<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> list_dynamic_symbols library_path [additional_nm_options]</span>
<span class="pl-en">list_dynamic_symbols</span>() {
<span class="pl-k">local</span> library=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">shift</span> 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
[ <span class="pl-k">-z</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$library</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> { <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>library not passed.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1<span class="pl-k">;</span> }<span class="pl-k">;</span>
nm --dynamic --extern-only --defined-only --demangle <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$@</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$library</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> list_static_symbols library_path [additional_nm_options]</span>
<span class="pl-en">list_static_symbols</span>() {
<span class="pl-k">local</span> library=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">shift</span> 1<span class="pl-k">;</span>
[ <span class="pl-k">-z</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$library</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> { <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>library not passed.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1<span class="pl-k">;</span> }<span class="pl-k">;</span>
nm --demangle --defined-only <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$@</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$library</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
}


<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> list_library_dependencies library_path recursive</span>
<span class="pl-en">list_library_dependencies</span>() {
<span class="pl-k">local</span> library=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">local</span> recursive=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$2</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">shift</span> 2<span class="pl-k">;</span>
[ <span class="pl-k">-z</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$library</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ] <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> { <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>library not passed.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1<span class="pl-k">;</span> }<span class="pl-k">;</span>
<span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$recursive</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>|<span class="pl-k">*</span>[!0-1]<span class="pl-k">*</span>) <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>recursive '<span class="pl-smi">$recursive</span>' passed is invalid. It must be 0 or 1.<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> 1;;<span class="pl-k">esac</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> [ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$recursive</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>0<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span> readelf --dynamic -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$library</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -F <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>(NEEDED)<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>  <span class="pl-k">|</span> sed -E <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/^.*Shared library: \[(.*)\]$/\1/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> ldd -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$library</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">fi</span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"> </h2><a id="user-content--6" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink:  " href="#-6"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p> </p>
<p><strong>Examples</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Search `foo.so` dynamic library in both `$TERMUX__PREFIX` and `/system/lib[64]` paths
search_dynamic_library foo.so 3

# Search `foo.a` static library in only `$TERMUX__PREFIX`
search_static_library foo.a 1

# Search `bar` dynamic library symbol in both `$TERMUX__PREFIX` and `/system/lib[64]` paths
search_dynamic_symbol &quot;bar&quot; 3

# Search `bar` static library symbol in only `/system/lib[64]` paths
search_static_symbol &quot;bar&quot; 2

# List `libtermux-api.so` dynamic library symbols
list_dynamic_symbols &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libtermux-api.so&quot;

# List `libtermux-api.a` static library symbols
list_static_symbols &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libtermux-api.a&quot;

# List `bash` direct dynamic library dependencies
list_library_dependencies &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin/bash&quot; 0

# List `bash` recursive dynamic library dependencies
list_library_dependencies &quot;$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin/bash&quot; 1"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Search `foo.so` dynamic library in both `$TERMUX__PREFIX` and `/system/lib[64]` paths</span>
search_dynamic_library foo.so 3

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Search `foo.a` static library in only `$TERMUX__PREFIX`</span>
search_static_library foo.a 1

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Search `bar` dynamic library symbol in both `$TERMUX__PREFIX` and `/system/lib[64]` paths</span>
search_dynamic_symbol <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>bar<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 3

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Search `bar` static library symbol in only `/system/lib[64]` paths</span>
search_static_symbol <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>bar<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 2

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> List `libtermux-api.so` dynamic library symbols</span>
list_dynamic_symbols <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$TERMUX__PREFIX</span>/lib/libtermux-api.so<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> List `libtermux-api.a` static library symbols</span>
list_static_symbols <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$TERMUX__PREFIX</span>/lib/libtermux-api.a<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> List `bash` direct dynamic library dependencies</span>
list_library_dependencies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$TERMUX__PREFIX</span>/bin/bash<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 0

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> List `bash` recursive dynamic library dependencies</span>
list_library_dependencies <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$TERMUX__PREFIX</span>/bin/bash<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> 1</pre></div>
<hr>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element">Path Environment Variables</h2><a id="user-content-path-environment-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Path Environment Variables" href="#path-environment-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>The <code>$HOME</code> variable is for the user's home directory. (<a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages/environ.7.en.html#HOME" rel="nofollow">1</a>)</p>
<p>The <code>$PATH</code>, <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> and <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> variables are part of the environment of processes/shells on Unix-like systems. (<a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages/environ.7.en.html" rel="nofollow">1</a>, <a href="https://pubs.opengroup.org/onlinepubs/9699919799/basedefs/V1_chap08.html" rel="nofollow">2</a>)</p>
<p>The <code>$PATH</code> variable is for the list of directory paths separated with colons <code>:</code> that certain functions and utilities use in searching for an executable file known only by a file <a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages-dev/basename.3.en.html" rel="nofollow"><code>basename</code></a>. The list of directory paths is searched from beginning to end, by checking the path formed by concatenating a directory path, a path separator <code>/</code>, and the executable file <code>basename</code>, and the first file found, if any, with execute permission is executed. (<a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages/environ.7.en.html#PATH" rel="nofollow">1</a>)</p>
<p>The <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> variable is for the list of directory paths separated with colons <code>:</code> that should be searched for dynamic/shared library files that are dependencies of executables or libraries to be linked against. The list of directory paths is searched from beginning to end, by checking the path formed by concatenating a directory path, a path separator <code>/</code>, and the library file <code>basename</code>, and the first file found, if any, with read permission is opened. (<a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages/ld.so.8.en.html#LD_LIBRARY_PATH" rel="nofollow">1</a>)</p>
<p>The <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> variable is for the list of ELF shared object paths separated with colons <code>:</code> to be loaded before all others. This feature can be used to selectively override functions in other shared objects. (<a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages/ld.so.8.en.html#LD_PRELOAD" rel="nofollow">1</a>)</p>
<hr>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element">Path Environment Variables Exported By Android</h2><a id="user-content-path-environment-variables-exported-by-android" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Path Environment Variables Exported By Android" href="#path-environment-variables-exported-by-android"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>Check <a href="./Termux-file-system-layout">Termux filesystem layout</a> docs (including <a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#android-paths">Android Paths</a> section) for more info on the Android filesystem directories.</p>
<p>The Android filesystem rootfs and home (<code>$HOME</code>) directory exists at <code>/</code>.</p>
<p>The Android system provided executables primarily exist under <code>/system/bin</code> that are part of AOSP itself that should exist on all devices depending on Android version as detailed by Android <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/system/core/+/master/shell_and_utilities/README.md" rel="nofollow"><code>shell_and_utilities</code></a> docs. The core utilities are primarily provided by <code>toybox</code> (<a href="http://landley.net/toybox" rel="nofollow">1</a>, <a href="https://github.com/landley/toybox">2</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:external/toybox" rel="nofollow">3</a>) for Android <code>&gt;= 6</code> and <code>toolbox</code> (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-5.0.0_r1.0.1:system/core/toolbox" rel="nofollow">1</a>) for Android <code>&lt; 6</code> and mostly have limited features compared to <code>GNU</code> <a href="https://www.gnu.org/software/coreutils/manual/coreutils.html" rel="nofollow"><code>coreutils</code></a> provided by Termux and other linux distros, like <a href="https://www.debian.org" rel="nofollow"><code>debian</code></a>. Moreover, older android versions do not have all the utilities or their features are missing or are severely broken. Additional apex, vendor or product partition specific (<a href="https://source.android.com/docs/core/architecture/partitions" rel="nofollow">1</a>, <a href="https://source.android.com/docs/core/ota/apex" rel="nofollow">2</a>, <a href="https://source.android.com/docs/core/architecture/partitions/product-partitions" rel="nofollow">3</a>), or custom ROM specific executables may exist under additional paths like  <code>/apex</code>, <code>/vendor</code>, <code>/product</code> or under <code>/sbin</code> and <code>/system/xbin</code> directories.</p>
<p>The Android system provided shared libraries exist under <code>/system/lib64</code> and/or <code>/system/lib</code> (or instead under <code>/apex/*/lib</code>) depending on if Android is <code>64-bit</code> or <code>32-bit</code>. Additional libraries may exist under <code>/odm/lib[64]</code>, <code>/vendor/lib[64]</code>, <code>/data/asan/system/lib[64]</code>, <code>/data/asan/odm/lib[64]</code> and <code>/data/asan/vendor/lib[64]</code>. The executables compiled for Android system do not use <code>DT_RUNPATH</code> or <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code>, and rely on <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=3391" rel="nofollow"><code>linker</code> to search in default library paths</a> listed earlier. Check <a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages/ld.so.8.en.html" rel="nofollow"><code>ld.so</code></a> and <a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages-dev/dlopen.3.en.html" rel="nofollow"><code>dlopen</code></a> man page and <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/linker/linker.cpp;l=102-125" rel="nofollow">Android system linker (<code>/system/bin/linker[64]</code>) source</a> for more info.</p>
<p>The Android system does not provide any <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> library.</p>
<p>Check following source links for info for which other environmental variables are exported by Android via <code>init</code> startup.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:frameworks/base/core/java/android/os/Environment.java" rel="nofollow">https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:frameworks/base/core/java/android/os/Environment.java</a></li>
<li><a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:system/core/rootdir/init.environ.rc.in" rel="nofollow">https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:system/core/rootdir/init.environ.rc.in</a></li>
<li><a href="https://cs.android.com/android/_/android/platform/system/core/+/refs/tags/android-14.0.0_r1:rootdir/init.rc;l=1022" rel="nofollow">https://cs.android.com/android/_/android/platform/system/core/+/refs/tags/android-14.0.0_r1:rootdir/init.rc;l=1022</a></li>
<li><a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:packages/modules/SdkExtensions/derive_classpath/derive_classpath.cpp;l=147" rel="nofollow">https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:packages/modules/SdkExtensions/derive_classpath/derive_classpath.cpp;l=147</a></li>
<li><a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/libc/include/paths.h" rel="nofollow">https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/libc/include/paths.h</a></li>
</ul>
<p> </p>
<p>The Android system exports path variables with the following default values for shells started for <a href="https://developer.android.com/tools/adb" rel="nofollow"><code>adb</code></a> and for app environments depending on the Android version. For info on <code>$PATH</code>, <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code>, <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> environment variables, check <a href="#path-environment-variables">Path Environment Variables</a>.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<code>$HOME</code>: <code>/</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#android-rootfs-directory">1</a>)</li>
<li>
<code>$PATH</code>: (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#android-bin-directory">1</a>)
<ul>
<li>Android <code>&gt;= 11</code>: <code>/product/bin:/apex/com.android.runtime/bin:/apex/com.android.art/bin:/system_ext/bin:/system/bin:/system/xbin:/odm/bin:/vendor/bin:/vendor/xbin</code> (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-11.0.0_r1:bionic/libc/include/paths.h;l=50" rel="nofollow">1</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-14.0.0_r1:bionic/libc/include/paths.h;l=50" rel="nofollow">2</a>)</li>
<li>Android <code>&gt;= 10</code>: <code>/sbin:/system/sbin:/product/bin:/apex/com.android.runtime/bin:/system/bin:/system/xbin:/odm/bin:/vendor/bin:/vendor/xbin</code> (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-10.0.0_r1:bionic/libc/include/paths.h;l=50" rel="nofollow">1</a>)</li>
<li>Android<code> &gt;= 9</code>: <code>/sbin:/system/sbin:/system/bin:/system/xbin:/odm/bin:/vendor/bin:/vendor/xbin</code> (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-9.0.0_r1:bionic/libc/include/paths.h;l=41" rel="nofollow">1</a>)</li>
<li>Android<code> &gt;= 8</code>: <code>/sbin:/system/sbin:/system/bin:/system/xbin:/vendor/bin:/vendor/xbin</code> (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-8.0.0_r1:bionic/libc/include/paths.h;l=39" rel="nofollow">1</a>)</li>
<li>Android<code> &lt; 8</code>: <code>/sbin:/vendor/bin:/system/sbin:/system/bin:/system/xbin</code> (<a href="https://cs.android.com/android/platform/superproject/+/android-7.0.0_r1:bionic/libc/include/paths.h;l=37" rel="nofollow">1</a>, <a href="https://cs.android.com/android/_/android/platform/system/core/+/refs/tags/android-5.0.0_r1:rootdir/init.environ.rc.in;l=3" rel="nofollow">2</a>)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code>: Not set by default. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#android-lib-directory">1</a>)</li>
<li>
<code>$LD_PRELOAD</code>: Not set by default.</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<p> </p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element">Path Environment Variables Exported By Termux</h2><a id="user-content-path-environment-variables-exported-by-termux" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Path Environment Variables Exported By Termux" href="#path-environment-variables-exported-by-termux"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>Check <a href="./Termux-file-system-layout">Termux filesystem layout</a> docs (including <a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-paths">Termux Paths</a> and <a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#file-path-limits">File Path Limits</a> sections) and <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/blob/master/scripts/properties.sh"><code>properties.sh</code></a> file for more info on the Termux filesystem directories and variables.</p>
<p>As mentioned in the <a href="#execution">Execution</a> section, termux packages <strong>are specifically compiled for the Termux <code>rootfs</code> directory <code>/data/data/com.termux/files</code> (<code>$TERMUX__ROOTFS</code>), based on the Termux app package name <code>com.termux</code> and the expected <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo#dataDir" rel="nofollow">private app data directory</a> <code>/data/data/com.termux</code></strong> android would assign to the app on installation if its installed on the primary user <code>0</code> of the device, as that would be the only directory that an app can access and place its files in and execute files from, which are also kept private from other apps as well for security reasons, The app data directory path assigned by Android will be different if the app package name is changed, or app is installed on a <a href="https://source.android.com/docs/devices/admin/multi-user" rel="nofollow">secondary user</a>, <a href="https://developer.android.com/work/managed-profiles" rel="nofollow">work profile</a> or <a href="https://source.android.com/docs/core/storage/adoptable" rel="nofollow">adoptable storage</a> and so <strong>Termux app must be installed in primary user <code>0</code></strong>, unless all its packages are re-compiled for the changes done.</p>
<p>The Termux provided executables currently primarily exist under <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin</code> (<code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin</code>). Some packages, like <code>busybox</code>, may have their executables under <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/applets</code> (<code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin/applets</code>). The core utilities are provided by <code>GNU</code> <a href="https://www.gnu.org/software/coreutils/manual/coreutils.html" rel="nofollow"><code>coreutils</code></a> to have a consistent experience with other linux distros, like <a href="https://www.debian.org" rel="nofollow"><code>debian</code></a>.</p>
<p>The Termux provided shared libraries exist under <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib</code> (<code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib</code>). The executables are compiled with <code>DT_RUNPATH</code> for Android <code>&gt;= 7</code> and do not use <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code>. For Android <code>5</code> and <code>6</code>, <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> is used. The <code>RUNPATH</code> value can be checked with <code>readelf -d $TERMUX__PREFIX/bin/&lt;executable&gt;</code>. Check <a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages/ld.so.8.en.html" rel="nofollow"><code>ld.so</code></a> and <a href="https://manpages.debian.org/testing/manpages-dev/dlopen.3.en.html" rel="nofollow"><code>dlopen</code></a> man page, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/blob/83e3271c/scripts/build/toolchain/termux_setup_toolchain_26b.sh#L34"><code>termux-packages</code> build infrastructure <code>termux_setup_toolchain</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/commit/c508560e"><code>c508560e</code></a>, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/commit/b997c4ea"><code>b997c4ea</code></a>), <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/blob/3b316cfc1782dbe004be880327f98a69e04e573d/packages/libllvm/clang-lib-Driver-ToolChains-Linux.cpp.patch#L32-L41">termux <code>clang</code> package</a> (<a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/commit/a4a2aa58"><code>a4a2aa58</code></a>, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/commit/d3f8fea1"><code>d3f8fea1</code></a>, <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/commit/3b316cfc"><code>3b316cfc</code></a>), <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-packages/blob/83e3271c8cf7e11b02ad2a7485dc64a8f6ea89b6/scripts/build/termux_step_massage.sh#L60-L64"><code>termux-packages</code> build infrastructure <code>termux-elf-cleaner</code></a> and <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-elf-cleaner/blob/v2.2.1/elf-cleaner.cpp#L167"><code>termux-elf-cleaner</code> source</a> (<a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-elf-cleaner/commit/623f314c"><code>623f314c</code></a>) for more info.</p>
<p>The Termux provided <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> library implemented by <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-exec"><code>termux-exec</code></a> exists at <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libtermux-exec.so</code> (<code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/lib/libtermux-exec.so</code>).</p>
<p>Check following source links for info for which other environmental variables are exported by Termux app via <code>TermuxShellEnvironment.getEnvironment()</code> method.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/termux/shell/command/environment/TermuxShellEnvironment.java">https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/termux/shell/command/environment/TermuxShellEnvironment.java</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/termux/shell/command/environment/TermuxAppShellEnvironment.java">https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/termux/shell/command/environment/TermuxAppShellEnvironment.java</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/termux/shell/command/environment/TermuxShellCommandShellEnvironment.java">https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/termux/shell/command/environment/TermuxShellCommandShellEnvironment.java</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/shell/command/environment/ShellCommandShellEnvironment.java">https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/shell/command/environment/ShellCommandShellEnvironment.java</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/shell/command/environment/AndroidShellEnvironment.java">https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/shell/command/environment/AndroidShellEnvironment.java</a></li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/shell/command/environment/UnixShellEnvironment.java">https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/master/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/shell/command/environment/UnixShellEnvironment.java</a></li>
</ul>
<p>The Termux app via <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-app/blob/f102ea20/termux-shared/src/main/java/com/termux/shared/termux/shell/command/environment/TermuxShellEnvironment.java#L41-L48"><code>TermuxShellEnvironment</code></a> class exports the <code>$PATH</code> and <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code> variables for shells started with the following default values. The <a href="https://github.com/termux/termux-tools/blob/v1.40.5/scripts/login.in#L42-L45"><code>$TERMUX__PREFIX/bin/login</code></a> script exports the <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> variable currently and is the only core variable that is not exported by the Termux app. For info on <code>$PATH</code>, <code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code>, <code>$LD_PRELOAD</code> environment variables, check <a href="#path-environment-variables">Path Environment Variables</a>.</p>
<p>The following <code>$TERMUX__</code> scoped variables are for the currently running Termux rootfs/app environment and <strong>should not be changed by programs</strong> and are only available for Termux app version <code>&gt;= 0.119.0</code>.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<code>$TERMUX_APP__DATA_DIR</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-private-app-data-directory">1</a>) (Added in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$TERMUX__PROJECT_DIR</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/termux</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-project-directory">1</a>) (Added in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$TERMUX__CORE_DIR</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/termux/core</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-core-directory">1</a>) (Added in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$TERMUX__APPS_DIR</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/termux/apps</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-apps-directory">1</a>) (Added in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$TERMUX__CACHE_DIR</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/cache</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-app-cache-directory">1</a>) (Added in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$TERMUX__ROOTFS</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-rootfs-directory">1</a>) (Added in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$TERMUX__HOME</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/home</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-home-directory">1</a>) (Added in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$HOME</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/home</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-home-directory">1</a>)</li>
<li>
<code>$TERMUX__PREFIX</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-prefix-directory">1</a>) (Added in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$PREFIX</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr</code>. (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-prefix-directory">1</a>) (Deprecated in Termux app <code>v0119.0</code>)</li>
<li>
<code>$PATH</code>: (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-bin-directory">1</a>)
<ul>
<li>Android <code>&gt;= 7</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin</code>
</li>
<li>Android <code>&lt; 7</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin:/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/applets</code>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<code>$LD_LIBRARY_PATH</code>: (<a href="./Termux-file-system-layout#termux-lib-directory">1</a>)
<ul>
<li>Android <code>&gt;= 7</code>: Not set by default.</li>
<li>Android <code>&lt; 7</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib</code>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<code>$LD_PRELOAD</code>: <code>/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/lib/libtermux-exec.so</code>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<p> </p>

              </div>

          </div>
</div>
